SUBENT        23620001   20250604                             23212362000100001 
BIB                 15         68                                 2362000100002 
TITLE      241Am Neutron Capture Cross Section Measurement using  2362000100003 
           the NaI(Tl) spectrometer of the ANNRI beamline of      2362000100004 
           J-PARC                                                 2362000100005 
AUTHOR     (G.Rovira,A.Kimura,S.Nakamura,S.Endo,O.Iwamoto,        2362000100006 
           N.Iwamoto,T.Katabuchi,Y.Kodama,H.Nakano,Y.Sato)        2362000100007 
INSTITUTE  (2JPNJAE,2JPNTIT)                                      2362000100008 
REFERENCE  (J,NST,61,459,2024)                                    2362000100009 
           #doi:10.1080/00223131.2023.2239885                     2362000100010 
FACILITY   (SYNCH,2JPNJAE) ANNRI(BL04) beamline of MLF at J-PARC  2362000100011 
REL-REF    (I,,K.Kino+,J,NIM/A,736,66,2014)                       2362000100012 
           Energy resolution of the pulsed neutron                2362000100013 
METHOD     (TOF,PHWT) Flight path length of 27.9 m.               2362000100014 
           Pulse-height weighting technique was applied.          2362000100015 
DETECTOR   (NAICR)                                                2362000100016 
           -Size: 330 mm (diam.) and 203 mm in thickness          2362000100017 
           -Angle: 90 deg with respect to the neutron beam line   2362000100018 
           -Flight length: 27.9 m                                 2362000100019 
           -DAQ: CAEN V1720 Digitizer (12bit, 250MHz)             2362000100020 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL) Spallation reaction in a mercury target        2362000100021 
           irradiated with 3-GeV protons (700 kW) .               2362000100022 
           The proton beams were supplied at a repetition rate    2362000100023 
           of 25 Hz and in the "double-bunch mode", in which      2362000100024 
           the pulsed protons consist of two bunches, each with   2362000100025 
           a width of 100 ns, at intervals of 600 ns.             2362000100026 
           Produced neutrons were slowed down in a supercritical  2362000100027 
           para-hydrogen moderator.                               2362000100028 
           A Disk chopper with a semicircular shape was used to   2362000100029 
           cut the low-energy tail of the neutron pulse.          2362000100030 
INC-SPECT  The neutron spectrum was reconstructed using the 478   2362000100031 
           keV gamma-rays from gamma rays from 10B(n,alpha        2362000100032 
           gamma) 7Li reaction.                                   2362000100033 
SAMPLE     7.47 +- 0.01 mg of 241Am oxide powder (957 MBq) mixed  2362000100034 
           with 46.0 mg of Y2O3 powder (binder) .                 2362000100035 
           Sample powder was pressed into a pellet shape with a   2362000100036 
           diameter 10 mm, and sealed in an Al case (an area      2362000100037 
           density of 2.37 x 10E-5 atoms/b) .                     2362000100038 
           A replica of the dummy case was used in order to       2362000100039 
           derive the sample-dependent background induced by      2362000100040 
           the case and the Y2O3.                                 2362000100041 
           A natural carbon sample was used as a neutron scatterer2362000100042 
           to derive the background due to scattered neutrons.    2362000100043 
           A thick gold sample with a diameter of 10.0 +- 0.1 mm  2362000100044 
           and a thickness of 0.10 +- 0.01 mm was employed for    2362000100045 
           normalization with the saturated resonance method.     2362000100046 
           A 90.4%-enriched boron sample with a mass of 86.3 mg,  2362000100047 
           and a diameter of 10.0 +- 0.1 mm was used for neutron  2362000100048 
           spectrum measurement.                                  2362000100049 
ANALYSIS   Pulse-height weighting technique (PHWT) was applied.   2362000100050 
           Measurements with the carbon sample,                   2362000100051 
           "Dummy replica sample", "carbon sample" and "Blank (no 2362000100052 
           sample) " were used for back ground estimation.        2362000100053 
           The relative neutron spectrum was estimated using      2362000100054 
           the boron sample.                                      2362000100055 
           The weighting function was normalized using the        2362000100056 
           saturated resonance method at the 1st resonance        2362000100057 
           of the gold sample.                                    2362000100058 
CORRECTION Dead Time Correction was applied with the non-         2362000100059 
           paralyzable model (deadtime: 1.25 +-0.01 us) .         2362000100060 
           Correction factors for self-shielding and multiple     2362000100061 
           scattering were deduced using the Monte-Carlo          2362000100062 
           simulation code PHITS.                                 2362000100063 
           Influence of the fission events were deduced and       2362000100064 
           subtracted using the 241Am capture and fission         2362000100065 
           cross sections and the gamma-ray multiplicities        2362000100066 
           for the capture and fission reactions.                 2362000100067 
HISTORY    (20250528R) Numerical data was obtained from AUTHOR.   2362000100068 
           (20250604C) Compiled by A. Kimura.                     2362000100069 
STATUS     (APRVD) Proofread by G. Rovira. (2025-06-04)           2362000100070

           (ERR-2) Systematic uncertainty due to                  2362000200008 
           frame-overlap subtraction.                             2362000200009 
           (ERR-3) Systematic uncertainty due to neutron flux.    2362000200010 
           (ERR-4) Systematic uncertainty due to normalization.   2362000200011 
           (ERR-5) Systematic uncertainty due to                  2362000200012 
           self-shielding and multiple scattering correction.     2362000200013 
           (ERR-6) Systematic uncertainty due to                  2362000200014 
           the determination of the weighting functions.          2362000200015

           Resonance energies, neutron and radiation widths       2362000400008 
           were determined with REFIT using Reich-Moor            2362000400009 
           approximation.                                         2362000400010 
           - The ANNRI beamline resolution function was taken     2362000400011 
           from the work of Kino. See REL-REF.                    2362000400012 
           - The initial resonance parametrization data           2362000400013 
           were taken from JENDL-5.                               2362000400014 
           - The initial delay and flight path were derived using 2362000400015 
           the results from the Au sample measurement.            2362000400016 
           - All resonances have been considered to be s-wave.    2362000400017 
           - Doppler effect was modeled using the                 2362000400018 
           free gas model with a temperature of 27 deg-C.         2362000400019 
           - Impurities were estimated from the fitting process   2362000400020 
           in the form of 1.52 +- 0.03 % of 237Np and             2362000400021 
           0.49 +- 0.08 % of 240Pu.                               2362000400022 
           - Simultaneous fitting results for the radiative width,2362000400023 
           neutron width were performed for 23 large resonances   2362000400024 
           below 18 eV.                                           2362000400025 
           The averaged radiation width was calculated as         2362000400026 
           44.7 +- 1.1 meV. This averaged radiation               2362000400027 
           width was used and kept fixed for the other resonances.2362000400028
